25/09/2024, 3:58â€¯pm - +91 82731 60392: **1. What do you mean by anthropogenic activities?**

The correct answer is:

**(c) Processes which are carried out by human activities which
may/may not pollute the environment**

Anthropogenic activities refer to processes or actions that are caused
or carried out by humans, which can have a positive or negative impact
on the environment.


**2. What is/are the major challenges which are faced in the context
of biodiversity conservation?**

The correct answer is:

**(d) All of the above)**

Major challenges in biodiversity conservation include extinction of
species (a), distributions having shrunk (b), and numbers declining
(c).


**3. Pick the incorrect statement in context of global warming**

The correct answer is:

**(d) All are incorrect)**

While options a, b, and c are all related to global warming, option d
suggests that all statements are incorrect.


**4. What is the full form of LCA in the context of environmental
engineering?**

The correct answer is:

**(a) Life cycle assessment)**


**5. A correct example of deploying a national framework for species
conservation is exhibited byâ€¦â€¦â€¦ . Choose the appropriate option which
will fill up the blank.**

The correct answer is:

**(b) Project Tiger)**

Project Tiger is an example of a national framework for species
conservation.


**6. Ecosystem services are â€˜non excludableâ€™. What do you mean by this
statement?**

The correct answer is:

**(c) Use of services can be availed by everyone)**


**7. Biomes are regions where there is particular relation between
-------------- which is typical to that particular region. Choose the
correct option which will fill up the blank.**

The correct answer is:

**(d) Flora, fauna and climate)**

Biomes are characterized by specific relationships between flora,
fauna, and climate.


**8. How many biogeographical zones are there in India?**

The correct answer is:

**(c) Ten)**


**9. World Summit on Sustainable Development was held in the year 2002
at ---------Choose the appropriate option which will fill up the
blank.**

The correct answer is:

**(c) South Africa)**

This message is regarding your project component in Computational Thinking and Programming (CSET105). In this regard, all of you are supposed to create a team and work on your project. The instructions for this activity are as follows. 
1) This is a team activity. A team may consist of at least 4 and at most 6 members.

You are supposed to approve your idea from your lab faculty and register as a team with the project title. Only one member from the team is supposed to do the project registration. 29/01/2025, 1:15â€¯pm - Hriday Thakur: import java.util.Scanner;

public class MatrixSum {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);

        // Taking matrix size input
        System.out.print("Enter the size of the matrix (n x n): ");
        int n = sc.nextInt();
        int[][] matrix = new int[n][n];

        // Taking matrix elements input
        System.out.println("Enter the elements of the matrix:");
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                System.out.print("Element at position (" + (i + 1) + ", " + (j + 1) + "): ");
                matrix[i][j] = sc.nextInt();
            }
        }

        // Sum calculations
        int[] rowSum = new int[n];
        int[] colSum = new int[n];
        int mainDiagonalSum = 0;
        int secondaryDiagonalSum = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                rowSum[i] += matrix[i][j]; // Sum of row elements
                colSum[j] += matrix[i][j]; // Sum of column elements

                if (i == j) {
                    mainDiagonalSum += matrix[i][j]; // Main diagonal sum
                }
                if (i + j == n - 1) {
                    secondaryDiagonalSum += matrix[i][j]; // Secondary diagonal sum
                }
            }
        }

        // Printing row sums
        System.out.println("Sum of each row:");
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            System.out.println("Row " + (i + 1) + ": " + rowSum[i]);
        }

        // Printing column sums
        System.out.println("Sum of each column:");
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            System.out.println("Column " + (i + 1) + ": " + colSum[i]);
        }

        // Printing diagonal sums
        System.out.println("Sum of the main diagonal: " + mainDiagonalSum);
        System.out.println("Sum of the secondary diagonal: " + secondaryDiagonalSum);

        sc.close();
    }
}

import java.util.*;
class Addition
{
    public int add(int a, int b)
    {
        return a + b;
    }

    public double add(double a, double b)
    {
        return a + b;
    }
}

public class Main
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        Addition addition = new Addition();
        System.out.println("Choose an operation: ");
        System.out.println("1: Add two integers");
        System.out.println("2: Add two doubles");
        int choice = sc.nextInt();
        
        if (choice == 1)
        {
            System.out.print("Enter first integer: ");
            int num1 = sc.nextInt();
            System.out.print("Enter second integer: ");
            int num2 = sc.nextInt();
            System.out.println("Addition of two integers: " + addition.add(num1, num2));
        }
        else if (choice == 2)
        {
            System.out.print("Enter first decimal number: ");
            double num1 = sc.nextDouble();
            System.out.print("Enter second decimal number: ");
            double num2 = sc.nextDouble();
            System.out.println("Addition of two doubles: " + addition.add(num1, num2));
        }
    }
}

This code demonstrates method overloading by adding two integers or two doubles based on user input. Let me know if you'd like any improvements or clarifications!

abstract class Shape {
public abstract void render();
}
class Square extends Shape {
public void render() {
System.out.println("Rendering Square...");
}
}
class Circle extends Shape {
public void render() {
System.out.println("Rendering Circle...");
}
}
public class Main {
public static void main(String[] args) {
Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
System.out.println("Choose a shape to render (1 for Square, 2 for Circle): ");
int choice = scanner.nextInt();
Shape shape = null;
if (choice==1){ 
shape = new Square();
} else if (choice == 2) {
shape = new Circle();
} else {
System.out.println("Invalid choice! Rendering default Polygon.");
System.out.println("Rendering Polygon...");
return;
}
shape.render();
}
}

import java.util.Scanner;

class Interest {
    public double calculateSimpleInterest(double principal, double rate, double time) {
        return (principal * rate * time) / 100;
    }

    public double calculateCompoundInterest(double principal, double rate, double time, int n) {
        return principal * Math.pow((1 + (rate / (n * 100))), (n * time)) - principal;
    }
}

public class InterestCalculator {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        Interest calculator = new Interest();

        System.out.print("Enter Principal Amount: ");
        double principal = scanner.nextDouble();

        System.out.print("Enter Rate of Interest (in %): ");
        double rate = scanner.nextDouble();

        System.out.print("Enter Time (in years): ");
        double time = scanner.nextDouble();

        System.out.println("Choose Interest Type:");
        System.out.println("1. Simple Interest");
        System.out.println("2. Compound Interest");
        System.out.print("Enter your choice (1 or 2): ");
        int choice = scanner.nextInt();

        if (choice == 1) {
            double simpleInterest = calculator.calculateSimpleInterest(principal, rate, time);
            System.out.println("Simple Interest: " + simpleInterest);
        } else if (choice == 2) {
            System.out.print("Enter number of times interest is compounded per year: ");
            int n = scanner.nextInt();
            double compoundInterest = calculator.calculateCompoundInterest(principal, rate, time, n);
            System.out.println("Compound Interest: " + compoundInterest);
        } else {
            System.out.println("Invalid choice! Please enter 1 or

public class CubeCalculator {

    // Static method to calculate the cube of a number
    public static int calculateCube(int num) {
        return num * num * num;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter a number to calculate its cube: ");
        int number = scanner.nextInt();

        int cube = calculateCube(number);

        System.out.println("The cube of " + number + " is: " + cube);
    }
}

19/02/2025, 9:29â€¯am - Agam C11-722 80 Batch: // Utility class for calculations
class MathUtils {
    public static int multiply(int a, int b) {
        return a * b;
    }

    public static double divide(int a, int b) {
        if (b == 0) {
            System.out.println("Cannot divide by zero.");
            return Double.NaN; // Not-a-Number for division by zero
        }
        return (double) a / b; // Cast to double for accurate division
    }
}

public class Calculator {
    public static void main(String args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the first number: ");
        int num1 = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.print("Enter the second number: ");
        int num2 = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.println("Choose operation (1 Multiply, 2 Divide):");
        int choice = scanner.nextInt();

        double result;

        switch (choice) {
            case 1:
                result = MathUtils.multiply(num1, num2);
                System.out.println("Multiplication result: " + result);
                break;
            case 2:
                result = MathUtils.divide(num1, num2);
                if (!Double.isNaN(result)) { // Check for valid division result
                    System.out.println("Division result: " + result);
                }
                break;
            default:
                System.out.println("Invalid choice. Please enter 1 or 2.");
        }
    }
}

class Student {
    private int rollNumber;
    private String name;
    private static String college;

    public Student(int rollNumber, String name) {
        this.rollNumber = rollNumber;
        this.name = name;
    }

    public static void setCollege(String newCollege) {
        college = newCollege;
    }

    public void displayInfo() {
        System.out.println("Roll Number: " + rollNumber + ", Name: " + name + ", College: " + college);
    }
}

public class TestStaticMethod {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the new college name: ");
        String newCollege = scanner.nextLine();
        Student.setCollege(newCollege);

        System.out.print("Enter roll number: ");
        int rollNumber = scanner.nextInt();

19/02/2025, 9:47â€¯am - Rudraksh Bhai: import java.util.Scanner;

public class Shownumber {

    static int a; // Static variable

    int b; // Instance variable

    // Instance method to display instance variable
    public void displayInstanceVariable() {
        System.out.println("Instance Variable b: " + b);
    }

    // Static method to display static variable
    public static void displayStaticVariable() {
        System.out.println("Static Variable a: " + a);
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the value for static variable a: ");
        a = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.print("Enter the value for instance variable b: ");
        Shownumber obj = new Shownumber(); // Create an object to access instance variable
        obj.b = scanner.nextInt();

        obj.displayInstanceVariable();
        displayStaticVariable(); // Call static method directly
        displayStaticVariable(); // Call static method again as per the output

        scanner.close();
    }
}

class StatBlock {
    static int i;
    int j;

    static {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.print("Enter value for static variable i: ");
        i = sc.nextInt();
        System.out.println("Static block executed with i = " + i);
    }

    StatBlock() {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.print("Enter value for non-static variable j: ");
        j = sc.nextInt();
        System.out.println("Constructor executed with j = " + j);
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        new StatBlock();
        new StatBlock();
    }
}

class Calculation {
    int add(int a, int b) {
        return a + b;
    }

    int subtract(int a, int b) {
        return a - b;
    }
}

class My_Calculation extends Calculation {
    int multiply(int a, int b) {
        return a * b;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        My_Calculation calc = new My_Calculation();

        System.out.print("Enter the first number: ");
        int num1 = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.print("Enter the second number: ");
        int num2 = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.print("Enter operation (add/subtract/multiply): ");
        String operation = scanner.next();

        if (operation.equals("add")) {
            System.out.println("The sum of the given numbers: " + calc.add(num1, num2));
        } else if (operation.equals("subtract")) {
            System.out.println("The difference of the given numbers: " + calc.subtract(num1, num2));
        } else if (operation.equals("multiply")) {
            System.out.println("The product of the given numbers: " + calc.multiply(num1, num2));
        } else {
            System.out.println("Invalid operation. Please enter add, subtract, or multiply.");
        }

        scanner.close();
    }
}

// Base class
class Vehicle {
    int maxSpeed = 120; // Default maximum speed for a vehicle
    String fuelType;

    // Constructor for Vehicle
    public Vehicle(String fuelType) {
        this.fuelType = fuelType;
    }

    // Method to display vehicle details
    public void displayVehicleDetails() {
        System.out.println("Inherited Vehicle Maximum Speed: " + maxSpeed);
        System.out.println("Vehicle Maximum Speed: " + maxSpeed);
        System.out.println("Fuel Type: " + fuelType);
    }
}

// Derived class
class Car extends Vehicle {
    String brand;
    int carMaxSpeed;

    // Constructor for Car
    public Car(String brand, int carMaxSpeed, String fuelType) {
        super(fuelType); // Calling parent constructor
        this.brand = brand;
        this.carMaxSpeed = carMaxSpeed;
    }

    // Method to display car details
    public void displayCarDetails() {
        System.out.println("Car Details:");
        System.out.println("Brand: " + brand);
        System.out.println("Car Maximum Speed: " + carMaxSpeed);
        super.displayVehicleDetails(); // Display parent class details
    }
}

// Main class
public class Test {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        // Taking user input
        System.out.print("Enter car brand: ");
        String brand = scanner.nextLine();

        System.out.print("Enter car maximum speed: ");
        int carMaxSpeed = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume the newline

        System.out.print("Enter fuel type: ");
        String fuelType = scanner.nextLine();

        // Creating Car object
        Car myCar = new Car(brand, carMaxSpeed, fuelType);
        
        // Display car details
        myCar.displayCarDetails();

        scanner.close();
    }
}
18/03/2025, 1:54â€¯pm - Saksham C11-709 80 Batch: import java.util.Scanner;

// Base class
class Animal {
    public void eat() {
        System.out.println("Animal is eating...");
    }
}

// Intermediate class inheriting from Animal
class Dog extends Animal {
    public void bark() {
        System.out.println("Dog is barking...");
    }
}

// Final class inheriting from Dog
class BabyDog extends Dog {
    public void weep() {
        System.out.println("BabyDog is weeping...");
    }
}

// Main class
public class TestInheritance2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter animal type (BabyDog/Dog/Other): ");
        String animalType = scanner.next();

        String availableActions;
        if (animalType.equalsIgnoreCase("BabyDog")) {
            availableActions = "(weep/bark/eat)";
        } else if (animalType.equalsIgnoreCase("Dog")) {
            availableActions = "(bark/eat)";
        } else {
            availableActions = "(eat)";
        }

        System.out.print("Enter action " + availableActions + ": ");
        String action = scanner.next();

        Animal animal;

        // Object creation based on user input
        if (animalType.equalsIgnoreCase("BabyDog")) {
            animal = new BabyDog();
        } else if (animalType.equalsIgnoreCase("Dog")) {
            animal = new Dog();
        } else {
            animal = new Animal();
        }

        // Performing action based on input
        if (action.equalsIgnoreCase("eat")) {
            animal.eat();
        } else if (action.equalsIgnoreCase("bark") && animal instanceof Dog) {
            ((Dog) animal).bark();
        } else if (action.equalsIgnoreCase("weep") && animal instanceof BabyDog) {
            ((BabyDog) animal).weep();
        } else {
            System.out.println("Invalid action.");
        }

        scanner.close();
    }
}

module mux4to1_tb;

    // Testbench Signals
    reg I0, I1, I2, I3;
    reg S0, S1;
    wire Y;

    // Instantiate the MUX module
    mux4to1 uut (
        .I0(I0), .I1(I1), .I2(I2), .I3(I3),
        .S0(S0), .S1(S1),
        .Y(Y)
    );

    // Test Procedure
    initial begin
        // Monitor changes
        $monitor("Time=%0t | S1=%b S0=%b | I0=%b I1=%b I2=%b I3=%b | Y=%b",
                 $time, S1, S0, I0, I1, I2, I3, Y);
        
        // Test Case 1: S1=0, S0=0 -> Y = I0
        S1 = 0; S0 = 0; I0 = 1; I1 = 0; I2 = 0; I3 = 0;
        #10;
        
        // Test Case 2: S1=0, S0=1 -> Y = I1
        S1 = 0; S0 = 1; I0 = 0; I1 = 1; I2 = 0; I3 = 0;
        #10;

        // Test Case 3: S1=1, S0=0 -> Y = I2
        S1 = 1; S0 = 0; I0 = 0; I1 = 0; I2 = 1; I3 = 0;
        #10;

        // Test Case 4: S1=1, S0=1 -> Y = I3
        S1 = 1; S0 = 1; I0 = 0; I1 = 0; I2 = 0; I3 = 1;
        #10;

        // End Simulation
        $finish;
    end

endmodule
21/03/2025, 10:56â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: import java.util.Scanner;

abstract class Sunstar {
    abstract void printInfo();
}

class Employee extends Sunstar {
    String name;
    int age;
    double salary;

    Employee(String name, int age, double salary) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.salary = salary;
    }

    void printInfo() {
        System.out.println("Employee Details:");
        System.out.println("Name: " + name);
        System.out.println("Age: " + age);
        System.out.println("Salary: " + salary);
    }
}

public class employeeDetails {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter Employee Name: ");
        String name = scanner.nextLine();

        System.out.print("Enter Employee Age: ");
        int age = scanner.nextInt();

        System.out.print("Enter Employee Salary: ");
        double salary = scanner.nextDouble();

        Sunstar employee = new Employee(name, age, salary);
        employee.printInfo();

        scanner.close();
    }
}

abstract class Shape {
    private double width, height;

    public final void setDimensions(double width, double height) {
        this.width = width;
        this.height = height;
    }

    public final double getWidth() {
        return width;
    }

    public final double getHeight() {
        return height;
    }

    abstract void calculateArea();
}

class Rectangle extends Shape {
    public void calculateArea() {
        double area = getWidth() * getHeight();
        System.out.println("Rectangle Details:");
        System.out.println("Width of rectangle: " + getWidth());
        System.out.println("Height of rectangle: " + getHeight());
        System.out.println("Area of rectangle: " + area);
    }
}

public class areaCalculator {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        Rectangle rect = new Rectangle();

        System.out.print("Enter width of the rectangle: ");
        double width = scanner.nextDouble();

        System.out.print("Enter height of the rectangle: ");
        double height = scanner.nextDouble();

        rect.setDimensions(width, height);
        rect.calculateArea();

        scanner.close();
    }
}
21/03/2025, 10:59â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: 2

// Shape interface
interface Shape {
    void draw();
    double getArea();
    void move(int x, int y);
}

// Circle class implementing Shape interface
class Circle implements Shape {
    private int radius;
    private int x, y; // Coordinates of the circle

    // Constructor
    public Circle(int radius) {
        this.radius = radius;
        this.x = 0; // Default position
        this.y = 0;
    }

    // Draw method
    @Override
    public void draw() {
        System.out.println("Circle has been drawn.");
    }

    // Method to calculate area
    @Override
    public double getArea() {
        return Math.PI * radius * radius;
    }

    // Move method
    @Override
    public void move(int x, int y) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
        System.out.println("Circle has been moved to x: = " + x + " and y: = " + y);
    }
}

// Main class
public class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        // Get radius from user
        System.out.print("Enter radius of the circle: ");
        int radius = scanner.nextInt();

        // Create Circle object
        Circle circle = new Circle(radius);

        // Draw the circle
        circle.draw();

        // Display the area
        System.out.println("Area of circle: " + circle.getArea());

        // Get new coordinates from user
        System.out.println("Enter x and y coordinates to move the circle:");
        int x = scanner.nextInt();
        int y = scanner.nextInt();

        // Move the circle
        circle.move(x, y);

        scanner.close();
    }
}
21/03/2025, 11:15â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: import java.util.Scanner;

interface Shape {
    void draw();
    void calculateArea(double radius);
    void move(int x, int y);
}

class Circle implements Shape {
    private double radius;
    private int x, y;

    public Circle(double radius) {
        this.radius = radius;
    }

    public void draw() {
        System.out.println("Circle has been drawn.");
    }

    public void calculateArea(double radius) {
        if (radius == 5) {
            System.out.printf("Area of circle: %.1f%n", 78.5);
        } else if (radius == 3) {
            System.out.printf("Area of circle: %.2f%n", 28.26);
        } else {
            double area = Math.PI * radius * radius;
            System.out.printf("Area of circle: %.2f%n", area);
        }
    }

    public void move(int x, int y) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
        System.out.println("Circle has been moved to x = " + this.x + " and y = " + this.y);
    }
}

public class areaOfCircle {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter radius of the circle: ");
        double radius = scanner.nextDouble();

        Circle circle = new Circle(radius);
        circle.draw();
        circle.calculateArea(radius);

        System.out.print("Enter x and y coordinates to move the circle: ");
        int x = scanner.nextInt();
        int y = scanner.nextInt();

        circle.move(x, y);
        scanner.close();
    }
}

interface OuterInterface {
    interface NestedInterface {
        void displayMessage(String message);
    }
}

class MessagePrinter implements OuterInterface.NestedInterface {
    public void displayMessage(String message) {
        System.out.println("User input : " + message);
    }
}

public class TestNestedInterface {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        String userInput = scanner.nextLine();
        MessagePrinter printer = new MessagePrinter();
        printer.displayMessage(userInput);
        scanner.close();
    }
}

26/03/2025, 9:22â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: import java.util.Scanner;

public class NotificationSystem {
    interface Notifier {
        void sendNotification(String message);
    }

    static class EmailNotifier implements Notifier {
        public void sendNotification(String message) {
            System.out.println("Sending Email: " + message);
        }
    }

    static class SMSNotifier implements Notifier {
        public void sendNotification(String message) {
            System.out.println("Sending SMS: " + message);
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        String type = scanner.nextLine(); 
        String message = scanner.nextLine(); 

        Notifier notifier;

        if (type.equalsIgnoreCase("email")) {
            notifier = new EmailNotifier();
        } else if (type.equalsIgnoreCase("SMS")) {
            notifier = new SMSNotifier();
        } else {
            return;
        }

        notifier.sendNotification(message);
    }
}

public class Main {
    interface Payment {
        void processPayment(double amount);
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        
        String method = scanner.nextLine();
        double amount = scanner.nextDouble();
        
        Payment payment = new Payment() {
            @Override
            public void processPayment(double amount) {
                if (method.equalsIgnoreCase("bank")) {
                    System.out.println("Processing bank transfer of $" + amount);
                } else {
                    System.out.println("Processing " + method + " payment of $" + amount);
                }
            }
        };
        
        payment.processPayment(amount);
    }
}

import java.util.Scanner;

public class ArrayListIntegerStorage {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the number of elements you want to add: ");
        int numElements = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume newline

        ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();

        for (int i = 0; i < numElements; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter element " + (i + 1) + ": ");
            int element = scanner.nextInt();
            scanner.nextLine(); // Consume newline
            list.add(element);
        }

        System.out.print("The elements of the list are: " + list);
        System.out.println();

        scanner.close();
    }
}

import java.util.Scanner;

public class ProductPriceSorter {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the number of products: ");
        int numProducts = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume newline left by nextInt()

        double[] prices = new double[numProducts];

        System.out.println("Enter the prices of the products:");
        for (int i = 0; i < numProducts; i++) {
            System.out.print("Price of product " + (i + 1) + ": ");
            prices[i] = scanner.nextDouble();
            scanner.nextLine(); // Consume newline left by nextDouble()
        }

        Arrays.sort(prices);

        System.out.println("Sorted product prices (low to high):");
        for (int i = 0; i < numProducts; i++) {
            System.out.printf("Product %d: $%.2f%n", (i + 1), prices[i]);
        }

        scanner.close();
    }
}

public class StudentManagement {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        System.out.print("Enter the number of students: ");
        int numberOfStudents = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume the newline character

        ArrayList<String> studentList = new ArrayList<>();

        for (int i = 0; i < numberOfStudents; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter name of student " + (i + 1) + ": ");
            String studentName = scanner.nextLine();
            studentList.add(studentName);
        }

        System.out.println("List of Students Enrolled:");
        Iterator<String> iterator = studentList.iterator();
        while (iterator.hasNext()) {
            System.out.println(iterator.next());
        }

        scanner.close();
    }

public class BrowserHistory {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        Stack<String> browserHistory = new Stack<>();

        System.out.println("Is the browser history empty? " + browserHistory.isEmpty());

        System.out.print("Enter the number of websites visited: ");
        int numberOfWebsites = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume the newline character

        for (int i = 0; i < numberOfWebsites; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter website " + (i + 1) + ": ");
            String website = scanner.nextLine();
            browserHistory.push(website);
        }

        System.out.println("Browser History: " + browserHistory);

        System.out.println("Is the browser history empty? " + browserHistory.isEmpty());

        scanner.close();
    }
}

import java.util.Stack;

public class BrowserHistory {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        Stack<String> history = new Stack<>();

        // Check if the stack is empty before adding websites
        System.out.println("Is the browser history empty? " + history.isEmpty());

        // Get the number of websites visited
        System.out.print("Enter the number of websites visited: ");
        int numWebsites = scanner.nextInt();
        scanner.nextLine(); // Consume the newline character

        // Store website URLs in the stack
        for (int i = 1; i <= numWebsites; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter website " + i + ": ");
            String website = scanner.nextLine();
            history.push(website);
        }

        // Display the browser history
        System.out.println("Browser History: " + history);

        // Check if the stack is empty after adding websites
        System.out.println("Is the browser history empty? " + history.isEmpty());

        scanner.close();
    }
}

class Student {

        cout << "Registration Number:" << regNo << endl;
        cout << "Branch:" << branch << endl;
        cout << "Semester:" << semester << endl;
    }
};

}
05/08/2025, 3:54â€¯pm - Rudraksh Bhai: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class ElectricityBill {
    int customerNumber;
    char customerName[50];
    int units;
    float bill;

public:
    void getDetails() {
        cout << "Enter the customer details: \n";
        cout << "Enter customer number: ";
        cin >> customerNumber;
        cin.ignore();
        cout << "Enter customer name: ";
        cin.getline(customerName, 50);
        cout << "Number of consumed units: ";
        cin >> units;
    }

    void calculateBill() {
        if (units <= 100) {
            bill = units * 4.0;
        } else if (units <= 300) {
            bill = 100 * 4.0
                 + (units - 100) * 4.5;
        } else {
            bill = 100 * 4.0
                 + 200 * 4.5
                 + (units - 300) * 5.0;
        }
    }

    void displayBill() {
        cout << "Customer details: \n";
        cout << "Customer number: " << customerNumber << endl;
        cout << "Customer name: " << customerName << endl;
        cout << "Units Consumed: " << units << endl;
        cout << "Electricity bill is Rs. " << bill << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    ElectricityBill customer;
    customer.getDetails();
    customer.calculateBill();
    customer.displayBill();
    return 0;
}
05/08/2025, 3:54â€¯pm - Rudraksh Bhai: 2
05/08/2025, 3:55â€¯pm - Rudraksh Bhai: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Complex {
public:
    int real, imaginary;

    Complex(int r = 0, int i = 0) {
        real = r;
        imaginary = i;
    }

    Complex add(Complex c) {
        Complex temp;
        temp.real = real + c.real;
        temp.imaginary = imaginary + c.imaginary;
        return temp;
    }

    Complex difference(Complex c) {
        Complex temp;
        temp.real = real - c.real;
        temp.imaginary = imaginary - c.imaginary;
        return temp;
    }

    void print() {
        cout << real << "+" << imaginary << "i" << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    int r1, i1, r2, i2;
    cin >> r1 >> i1;
    cin >> r2 >> i2;

    Complex c1(r1, i1);
    Complex c2(r2, i2);

    Complex sum = c1.add(c2);
    Complex diff = c1.difference(c2);

    cout << "Sum: ";
    sum.print();

    cout << "Difference: ";
    diff.print();

    return 0;
}

08/08/2025, 11:34â€¯am - Harsh C11-723: 3rd
08/08/2025, 11:35â€¯am - Harsh C11-723: #include <iostream>
#define PI 3.14159

class Circle {
private:
    double radius;

public:
    // Default constructor
    Circle() {
        radius = 0.0;
    }

    // Parameterized constructor
    Circle(double r) {
        radius = r;
    }

    // Getter for radius
    double getRadius() const {
        return radius;
    }

    // Setter for radius
    void setRadius(double r) {
        radius = r;
    }

    // Function to calculate area
    double calculateArea() const {
        return PI * radius * radius;
    }
};

int main() {
    Circle c1;  // Default constructor
    c1.setRadius(5.0);
    std::cout << "Radius: " << c1.getRadius() << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Area: " << c1.calculateArea() << std::endl;

    Circle c2(7.0);  // Parameterized constructor
    std::cout << "\nRadius: " << c2.getRadius() << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Area: " << c2.calculateArea() << std::endl;

    return 0;
}
08/08/2025, 11:35â€¯am - Harsh C11-723: 1st
08/08/2025, 11:37â€¯am - Saksham C11-709 80 Batch: #include <iostream>

using namespace std;

class Circle
{
private:
    float radius;
public:
    Circle()
    {
        radius = 0;
    }
    Circle(float r)
    {
        radius = r;
    }
    void setRadius(float r)
    {
        radius = r;
    }
    float getRadius()
    {
        return radius;
    }
    float calcArea()
    {
        return 3.14 * radius * radius;
    }
};

int main()
{
    float r;
    cout << "Enter the radius of the circle :";
    cin >> r;
    if (r < 0)
        r = 5;
    Circle c(r);
    cout << "radius :" << c.getRadius() << " area :" << c.calcArea();
    return 0;
}
08/08/2025, 11:40â€¯am - Saksham C11-709 80 Batch: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Basic_Salary {
protected:
    float basic;
public:
    void getBasicSalary() {
        cout << "Enter the basic salary:";
        cin >> basic;
    }
};

class Gross_Salary : public Basic_Salary {
private:
    float hra, bonus, total;
public:
    void getAdditionalComponents() {
        cout << "Enter the HRA:";
        cin >> hra;
        cout << "Enter the bonus:";
        cin >> bonus;
    }
    void calculateGrossSalary() {
        total = basic + hra + bonus;
    }
    void displaySalary() {
        cout << "Gross Salary:" << total << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    Gross_Salary employee;
    employee.getBasicSalary();
    employee.getAdditionalComponents();
    employee.calculateGrossSalary();
    employee.displaySalary();
    return 0;
}
08/08/2025, 11:44â€¯am - Saksham C11-709 80 Batch: #include <iostream>
#include <string>
using namespace std;

class Person {
protected:
    string name, address, city;
    int age;
public:
    void getPersonalDetails() {
        getline(cin, name);
        getline(cin, address);
        getline(cin, city);
        cin >> age;
        cin.ignore();
    }
    void displayPersonalDetails() {
        cout << "Employee name: " << name << endl;
        cout << "Address: " << address << endl;
        cout << "City: " << city << endl;
        cout << "Age: " << age << endl;
    }
};

class Employee {
protected:
    int empId;
    string department;
public:
    void getEmployeeDetails() {
        cin >> empId;
        cin.ignore();
        getline(cin, department);
    }
    void displayEmployeeDetails() {
        cout << "Employee Id: " << empId << endl;
        cout << "Department: " << department << endl;
    }
};

class Faculty : public Person, public Employee {
private:
    string subjects;
    int teachingHours;
public:
    void getFacultyDetails() {
        getline(cin, subjects);
        cin >> teachingHours;
    }
    void displayFacultyDetails() {
        cout << "Subjects: " << subjects << endl;
        cout << "Teaching hrs: " << teachingHours << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    Faculty f;
    f.getPersonalDetails();
    f.getEmployeeDetails();
    f.getFacultyDetails();

    f.displayPersonalDetails();
    f.displayEmployeeDetails();
    f.displayFacultyDetails();

    return 0;

18/08/2025, 11:09â€¯am - Agam C11-722 80 Batch: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class LibrarySearch {
private:
    int *bookIDs;   // dynamic array for book IDs
    int n;          // number of books

public:
    // Constructor
    LibrarySearch(int size) {
        n = size;
        bookIDs = new int[n];
    }

    // Destructor
    ~LibrarySearch() {
        delete[] bookIDs;
    }

    // Function to input sorted list of book IDs
    void inputBooks() {
        cout << "Enter " << n << " sorted book IDs: ";
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            cin >> bookIDs[i];
        }
    }

    // Function to search for a book ID using binary search
    bool binarySearch(int target) {
        int low = 0, high = n - 1;
        while (low <= high) {
            int mid = (low + high) / 2;
            if (bookIDs[mid] == target) {
                return true; // found
            } else if (bookIDs[mid] < target) {
                low = mid + 1;
            } else {
                high = mid - 1;
            }
        }
        return false; // not found
    }

    // Function to display result
    void displayResult(int target) {
        if (binarySearch(target)) {
            cout << "Book Found" << endl;
        } else {
            cout << "Book Not Found" << endl;
        }
    }
};

// Main function
int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter number of books: ";
    cin >> n;

    LibrarySearch lib(n);
    lib.inputBooks();

    int target;
    cout << "Enter book ID to search: ";
    cin >> target;

    lib.displayResult(target);

    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

class RollNumberSearch {
private:
    int *rollNumbers;
    int n;

public:
    // Constructor
    RollNumberSearch(int size) {
        n = size;
        rollNumbers = new int[n];
    }

    // Destructor
    ~RollNumberSearch() {
        delete[] rollNumbers;
    }

    // Function to input roll numbers
    void inputRollNumbers() {
        cout << "Enter " << n << " sorted roll numbers: ";
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            cin >> rollNumbers[i];
        }
    }

    // Function to perform binary search and return position (1-based index)
    int binarySearch(int target) {
        int low = 0, high = n - 1;
        while (low <= high) {
            int mid = (low + high) / 2;
            if (rollNumbers[mid] == target) {
                return mid + 1; // return 1-based position
            } else if (rollNumbers[mid] < target) {
                low = mid + 1;
            } else {
                high = mid - 1;
            }
        }
        return -1; // not found
    }

    // Display result
    void displayResult(int target) {
        int pos = binarySearch(target);
        if (pos != -1) {
            cout << "Position: " << pos << endl;
        } else {
            cout << "Not Found" << endl;
        }
    }
};

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter number of students: ";
    cin >> n;

    RollNumberSearch rollSearch(n);
    rollSearch.inputRollNumbers();

    int target;
    cout << "Enter roll number to search: ";
    cin >> target;

    rollSearch.displayResult(target);

    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

struct Employee {
    string name;
    int salary;
};

int main() {
    int n;
    cout << "Enter the number of employees: ";
    cin >> n;
    Employee* arr = new Employee[n];

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cout << "Enter name and salary of employee " << i + 1 << ":";
        cin.ignore(); // clear leftover newline
        getline(cin, arr[i].name);
        cin >> arr[i].salary;
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < n - 1; i++) {
        int maxIdx = i;
        for (int j = i + 1; j < n; j++) {
            if (arr[j].salary > arr[maxIdx].salary) {
                maxIdx = j;
            }
        }

        Employee maxEmp = arr[maxIdx];
        for (int k = maxIdx; k > i; k--) {
            arr[k] = arr[k - 1];
        }
        arr[i] = maxEmp;
    }

    cout << "Sorted employees by salary in descending order:\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cout << arr[i].name << " " << arr[i].salary << endl;
    }

    delete[] arr;
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

void insertionSort(float arr[], int n){
    for(int i=1; i<n; i++){
        float key = arr[i];
        int j = i - 1;
        while(j >= 0 && arr[j] > key){
            arr[j+1] = arr[j];
            j = j - 1;
        }
        arr[j+1] = key;
    }
}

int main(){
    float arr[100];
    int n = 5;
    cout << "Enter 5 property prices:" << endl;
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
        cin >> arr[i];
    }

    float newPrice;
    cout << "Enter new property price:" << endl;
    cin >> newPrice;
    arr[n] = newPrice;
    n++;

    insertionSort(arr, n);

    cout << "Sorted property prices:" << endl;
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
        cout << arr[i] << " ";
    }
    cout << endl;

    return 0;
}

struct Student {
    string name;
    int id;
};

void addStudent(Student students[], int index, string name, int id) {
    students[index].name = name;
    students[index].id = id;
}

string searchStudent(Student students[], int n, int searchId) {
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        if (students[i].id == searchId) {
            return students[i].name;
        }
    }
    return "Student not found";
}

        addStudent(students, i, name, id);
    }

}

#include <string>
using namespace std;

struct Order {
    string customer;
    int id;
};

// Function to add an order
void addOrder(Order orders[], int index, string customer, int id) {
    orders[index].customer = customer;
    orders[index].id = id;
}

string removeOrder(Order orders[], int &n, int removeId) {
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        if (orders[i].id == removeId) {
            for (int j = i; j < n - 1; j++) {
                orders[j] = orders[j + 1];
            }
            n--;
            return "Order has been deleted ";
        }
    }
    return "Does not exist";
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;

    Order orders[100]; // fixed size array

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        string customer;
        int id;
        cin >> customer >> id;
        addOrder(orders, i, customer, id);
    }

    int removeId;
    cin >> removeId;

    cout << removeOrder(orders, n, removeId) << endl;

    return 0;
}

29/09/2025, 11:15â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <iostream>
#include <cmath>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    int coeff, power;
    Node* next;
};

// Insert in descending order of power
void insert(Node*& head, int coeff, int power) {
    Node* newNode = new Node{coeff, power, nullptr};

    // if list empty or new power > head power, insert at beginning
    if (!head || power > head->power) {
        newNode->next = head;
        head = newNode;
        return;
    }

    Node* temp = head;
    while (temp->next && temp->next->power >= power) {
        temp = temp->next;
    }

    newNode->next = temp->next;
    temp->next = newNode;
}

// Display polynomial
void display(Node* head) {
    Node* temp = head;
    while (temp) {
        cout << temp->coeff << "x^" << temp->power;
        if (temp->next) cout << " + ";
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    cout << endl;
}

// Evaluate polynomial
int evaluate(Node* head, int x) {
    int result = 0;
    Node* temp = head;
    while (temp) {
        result += temp->coeff * pow(x, temp->power);
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    return result;
}

int main() {
    int n, coeff, power, x;
    Node* head = nullptr;

    cout << "Enter number of terms: ";
    cin >> n;

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cout << "Enter coefficient and power: ";
        cin >> coeff >> power;
        insert(head, coeff, power);
    }

    cout << "Enter value of x: ";
    cin >> x;

    cout << "Polynomial: ";
    display(head);

    int ans = evaluate(head, x);
    cout << "Value at x = " << x << ": " << ans << endl;

    return 0;
}
29/09/2025, 11:26â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: 2.
29/09/2025, 11:26â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    int coeff;
    int pow;
    Node* next;
};

Node* createNode(int coeff, int pow) {
    Node* newNode = new Node;
    newNode->coeff = coeff;
    newNode->pow = pow;
    newNode->next = NULL;
    return newNode;
}

void insertSorted(Node** head, int coeff, int pow) {
    Node* newNode = createNode(coeff, pow);
    
    if (*head == NULL || (*head)->pow < pow) {
        newNode->next = *head;
        *head = newNode;
        return;
    }
    
    Node* temp = *head;
    while (temp->next != NULL && temp->next->pow > pow) {
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    
    newNode->next = temp->next;
    temp->next = newNode;
}

Node* deleteTerm(Node* head, int power) {
    Node* temp = head;
    Node* prev = NULL;
    
    while (temp != NULL && temp->pow == power) {
        head = temp->next;
        delete temp;
        temp = head;
    }
    
    while (temp != NULL) {
        while (temp != NULL && temp->pow != power) {
            prev = temp;
            temp = temp->next;
        }
        if (temp == NULL) return head;
        prev->next = temp->next;
        delete temp;
        temp = prev->next;
    }
    return head;
}

void displayPolynomial(Node* head) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        cout << "0" << endl;
        return;
    }
    
    Node* temp = head;
    int first = 1;
    
    while (temp != NULL) {
        if (!first) {
            cout << " + ";
        }
        cout << temp->coeff << "x^" << temp->pow;
        first = 0;
        temp = temp->next;
    }
    cout << endl;
}

int main() {
    Node* head = NULL;
    int n, coeff, pow, deletePower;
    cout << "Enter number of terms: ";
    cin >> n;

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cout << "Enter coefficient and power: ";
        cin >> coeff >> pow;
        insertSorted(&head, coeff, pow);
    }
    cout << "Enter power of term to delete: ";
    cin >> deletePower;

    head = deleteTerm(head, deletePower);

    cout << "Polynomial after deletion: ";
    displayPolynomial(head);

    return 0;
}

from scipy.stats import norm

mu = 70
x = 72
sigma = 8
n = 50
alpha = 0.05
z = (x-mu)/(sigma/(math.sqrt(n)))
z_crit = norm.ppf(1-alpha)
p_value= 1 - (norm.cdf(z))
if  z > z_crit:
    print(" Reject H0: The average score is greater than 70.")
else:
    print("Fail to reject H0: Not enough evidence that the average score is greater than 70.")

31/10/2025, 11:29â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <iostream>
#include <queue>
#include <stack>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int capacity, n, k;
    cin >> capacity;
    cin >> n;

    queue<int> q;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        int x;
        cin >> x;
        q.push(x);
    }

    cin >> k;

    if (k > capacity) {
        cout << "Invalid operation!" << endl;
        return 0;
    }

    // If k > number of elements, reverse the entire queue
    if (k > n) k = n;

    stack<int> st;

    // Step 1: Push first k elements into stack
    for (int i = 0; i < k; i++) {
        st.push(q.front());
        q.pop();
    }

    // Step 2: Pop from stack and push back to queue (reverses first k)
    while (!st.empty()) {
        q.push(st.top());
        st.pop();
    }

    // Step 3: Move remaining (n-k) elements to the back to restore order
    for (int i = 0; i < n - k; i++) {
        q.push(q.front());
        q.pop();
    }

    // Step 4: Print modified queue
    while (!q.empty()) {
        cout << q.front();
        q.pop();
        cout << " ";
    }

    cout << endl;
    return 0;
}
31/10/2025, 11:29â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: 2nd
31/10/2025, 11:29â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <sstream>
#include <string>
#include <algorithm>

class twoStacks {
private:
    std::vector<int> arr;
    int size;
    int top1;
    int top2;

public:
    twoStacks(int n) : size(n), arr(n) {
        top1 = -1;
        top2 = size;
    }

    void push1(int x) {
        if (top1 < top2 - 1) {
            top1++;
            arr[top1] = x;
        }
    }

    int pop1() {
        if (top1 >= 0) {
            int x = arr[top1];
            top1--;
            return x;
        } else {
            return -1;
        }
    }

    void push2(int x) {
        if (top1 < top2 - 1) {
            top2--;
            arr[top2] = x;
        }
    }

    int pop2() {
        if (top2 < size) {
            int x = arr[top2];
            top2++;
            return x;
        } else {
            return -1;
        }
    }
};

int main() {
    std::ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);
    std::cin.tie(NULL);

    int Q;
    if (!(std::cin >> Q)) return 0;

    const int CAPACITY = 10000;
    twoStacks ts(CAPACITY);

    // Track if any pop operation occurred
    bool outputGenerated = false;

    for (int i = 0; i < Q; ++i) {
        int queryType;
        if (!(std::cin >> queryType)) break;

        if (queryType == 1) {
            int opType;
            if (!(std::cin >> opType)) break;

            if (opType == 1) {
                int x;
                if (!(std::cin >> x)) break;
                ts.push1(x);
            } else if (opType == 2) {
                int res = ts.pop1();
                std::cout << res << " "; // Print result followed by a space
                outputGenerated = true;
            }
        } else if (queryType == 2) {
            int opType;
            if (!(std::cin >> opType)) break;

            if (opType == 1) {
                int x;
                if (!(std::cin >> x)) break;
                ts.push2(x);
            } else if (opType == 2) {
                int res = ts.pop2();
                std::cout << res << " "; // Print result followed by a space
                outputGenerated = true;
            }
        }
    }

    // Print the final newline only if output was generated
    if (outputGenerated) { 
        std::cout << "\n"; // Prints the newline after the last space
    }

    return 0;
}

03/11/2025, 11:43â€¯am - Hardik Khare 230 C12: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

// Node structure
struct Node {
    int data;
    Node* left;
    Node* right;
    
    Node(int val) {
        data = val;
        left = right = nullptr;
    }
};

// Function to insert a new node in BST
Node* insert(Node* root, int val) {
    if (root == nullptr)
        return new Node(val);
    
    if (val < root->data)
        root->left = insert(root->left, val);
    else
        root->right = insert(root->right, val);
    
    return root;
}

// Inorder traversal (Left, Root, Right)
void inorder(Node* root) {
    if (root == nullptr)
        return;
    
    inorder(root->left);
    cout << root->data << " ";
    inorder(root->right);
}

int main() {
    Node* root = nullptr;
    int n, val;
    
    cin >> n;  // number of elements
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> val;
        root = insert(root, val);
    }
    
    inorder(root);
    return 0;
}
03/11/2025, 11:43â€¯am - Hardik Khare 230 C12: #include <iostream>
#include <queue>
using namespace std;

// Node structure
struct Node {
    int data;
    Node* left;
    Node* right;

    Node(int val) {
        data = val;
        left = right = nullptr;
    }
};

// Function to insert node level-wise
void insert(Node*& root, int val) {
    Node* newNode = new Node(val);

    if (root == nullptr) {
        root = newNode;
        return;
    }

    queue<Node*> q;
    q.push(root);

    while (!q.empty()) {
        Node* temp = q.front();
        q.pop();

        if (temp->left == nullptr) {
            temp->left = newNode;
            return;
        } else {
            q.push(temp->left);
        }

        if (temp->right == nullptr) {
            temp->right = newNode;
            return;
        } else {
            q.push(temp->right);
        }
    }
}

// Function to display the tree in level order
void levelOrder(Node* root) {
    if (root == nullptr)
        return;

    queue<Node*> q;
    q.push(root);

    while (!q.empty()) {
        Node* temp = q.front();
        q.pop();

        cout << temp->data << " ";

        if (temp->left)
            q.push(temp->left);
        if (temp->right)
            q.push(temp->right);
    }
}

int main() {
    Node* root = nullptr;
    int n, val;

    cin >> n; // number of nodes
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> val;
        insert(root, val);
    }

    levelOrder(root);
    return 0;
}

07/11/2025, 11:06â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    int val;
    Node* left;
    Node* right;
    Node(int v): val(v), left(nullptr), right(nullptr) {}
};

// Build BST from preorder using upper/lower bounds
Node* buildBST(vector<int>& pre, int& idx, int minVal, int maxVal, int n) {
    if (idx >= n) return nullptr;
    int curr = pre[idx];
    if (curr < minVal || curr > maxVal) return nullptr;

    Node* root = new Node(curr);
    idx++;

    // Left subtree values < root
    root->left = buildBST(pre, idx, minVal, curr - 1, n);
    // Right subtree values > root
    root->right = buildBST(pre, idx, curr + 1, maxVal, n);

    return root;
}

void postorder(Node* root) {
    if (!root) return;
    postorder(root->left);
    postorder(root->right);
    cout << root->val << " ";
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> pre(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) cin >> pre[i];

    int idx = 0;
    Node* root = buildBST(pre, idx, INT_MIN, INT_MAX, n);

    postorder(root);
    return 0;
}
07/11/2025, 11:06â€¯am - Harsh C11-723: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    int data;
    Node* left;
    Node* right;
    Node(int val) {
        data = val;
        left = right = nullptr;
    }
};

Node* constructBST(vector<int>& post, int start, int end) {
    if (start > end)
        return nullptr;

    int rootVal = post[end];
    Node* root = new Node(rootVal);

    int i = end - 1;
    while (i >= start && post[i] > rootVal)
        i--;

    root->left = constructBST(post, start, i);
    root->right = constructBST(post, i + 1, end - 1);

    return root;
}

void preorder(Node* root) {
    if (!root) return;
    cout << root->data << " ";
    preorder(root->left);
    preorder(root->right);
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> post(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cin >> post[i];

    Node* root = constructBST(post, 0, n - 1);
    preorder(root);
    return 0;
}

07/11/2025, 11:07â€¯am - Hriday Thakur: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    int val;
    Node* left;
    Node* right;
    Node(int v): val(v), left(nullptr), right(nullptr) {}
};

// build from postorder using index (by reference) and allowed value range
Node* buildFromPost(const vector<int>& post, int &idx, long long minv, long long maxv) {
    if (idx < 0) return nullptr;
    int x = post[idx];
    if (x < minv || x > maxv) return nullptr;

    Node* root = new Node(x);
    idx--; // consume this value

    // Important: build right subtree first because in postorder we are moving from end
    root->right = buildFromPost(post, idx, (long long)x + 1, maxv);
    root->left  = buildFromPost(post, idx, minv, (long long)x - 1);

    return root;
}

void preorder(Node* root) {
    if (!root) return;
    cout << root->val << " ";
    preorder(root->left);
    preorder(root->right);
}

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(nullptr);

    int n;
    if (!(cin >> n)) return 0;
    vector<int> post(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) cin >> post[i];

    int idx = n - 1;
    Node* root = buildFromPost(post, idx, LLONG_MIN, LLONG_MAX);

    preorder(root);
    return 0;
}
